I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Regression in 2026.4.0: substitutions: !include file.yaml no longer works (worked in all previous versions)
### The problem

**Which version of ESPHome has the issue?**
2026.4.0

**Last working version:**
All versions before 2026.4.0

**What type of installation are you using?**
Manual / pip (ESPHome Studio by ATNEL)

**Describe the bug:**
The substitution system redesign in 2026.4.0 (PR #14918) introduced a regression.
The following syntax, which worked correctly in all previous versions, now fails:

substitutions: !include components/substitutions.yaml

Error message:
  Substitutions must be a key to value mapping, got <class 'esphome.helpers.IncludeFile'>

**Use case / Why this matters:**
This is a legitimate and widely used pattern for workspace-level shared substitution files.
Example architecture:

  workspace/
    EHSFONTS/
      mdi_glyph_substitutions.yaml   <-- shared across ALL projects (~7000 lines of MDI glyph definitions)
    project-A/
      project-A.yaml                 <-- substitutions: !include components/substitutions.yaml
      components/
        substitutions.yaml           <-- <<: !include ../../EHSFONTS/mdi_glyph_substitutions.yaml
    project-B/
      project-B.yaml
      components/
        substitutions.yaml

This pattern allows:
1. One shared glyph file for all projects (no duplication)
2. Per-project user substitutions in components/substitutions.yaml
3. Main YAML managed by a wizard/generator tool (user does not edit it directly)

Breaking this pattern forces either:
- Duplicating 7000 lines of glyph definitions into every single project
- Inlining substitutions into the wizard-managed main YAML (breaks the tool architecture)

**Minimal reproduction:**

File: mydevice.yaml
  substitutions: !include subs.yaml

File: subs.yaml
  my_variable: "hello"

**Expected behavior:**
Works as before - substitutions file is loaded and merged as a key-value map.

**Actual behavior:**
  Failed config
  substitutions: None
    {}
  Substitutions must be a key to value mapping, got <class 'esphome.helpers.IncludeFile'>

### Which version of ESPHome has the issue?

2026.4.0

### What type of installation are you using?

pip

### What platform are you using?

ESP8266

### Component causing the issue

substitutions

### YAML Config

```yaml
# Minimal reproduction - main file: mydevice.yaml
substitutions: !include components/substitutions.yaml

esphome:
  name: test-device

esp8266:
  board: d1_mini

# File: components/substitutions.yaml
<<: !include ../../EHSFONTS/mdi_glyph_substitutions.yaml


# File: EHSFONTS/mdi_glyph_substitutions.yaml (fragment)
mdi_ab_testing: "\U000F01C9"
mdi_abacus: "\U000F16E0"
# ... (thousands of MDI glyph definitions)
```

### Anything in the logs that might be useful for us?

```txt
INFO ESPHome 2026.4.0
INFO Reading configuration mydevice.yaml...
Failed config
substitutions: None
  {}
Substitutions must be a key to value mapping, got <class 'esphome.helpers.IncludeFile'>
```

### Additional information

This syntax worked correctly in all ESPHome versions before 2026.4.0.
The regression was introduced by the substitution system redesign in PR #14918.

Workspace structure used:
  workspace/
    EHSFONTS/
      mdi_glyph_substitutions.yaml   <-- ~7000 lines, shared across all projects
    project-A/
      project-A.yaml                 <-- substitutions: !include components/substitutions.yaml
      components/
        substitutions.yaml           <-- <<: !include ../../EHSFONTS/mdi_glyph_substitutions.yaml

This architecture allows one shared glyph file for all projects without duplication.
Breaking this forces copying 7000 lines into every single project - unacceptable.

</pr_description>

    33	def validate_substitution_key(value: Any) -> str:
    34	    """Validate and normalize a substitution key, stripping a leading ``$`` if present."""
    35	    value = cv.string(value)
    36	    if not value:
    37	        raise cv.Invalid("Substitution key must not be empty")
    38	    if value[0] == "$":
    39	        value = value[1:]
    40	    if not value:
    41	        raise cv.Invalid("Substitution key must not be empty")
    42	    if value[0].isdigit():
    43	        raise cv.Invalid("First character in substitutions cannot be a digit.")
    44	    for char in value:
    45	        if char not in VALID_SUBSTITUTIONS_CHARACTERS:
    46	            raise cv.Invalid(
    47	                f"Substitution must only consist of upper/lowercase characters,"
    48	                f" the underscore and numbers."
    49	                f" The character '{char}' cannot be used"
    50	            )
    51	    return value
    52

    55	    {
    56	        validate_substitution_key: object,
    57	    }

    61	async def to_code(config: ConfigType) -> None:
    62	    """No runtime code generation needed — substitutions are resolved at config time."""
    63	
    64	
    65	def _restore_data_base(value: Any, orig_value: ESPHomeDataBase) -> ESPHomeDataBase:
    66	    """This function restores ESPHomeDataBase metadata held by the original string.
    67	    This is needed because during jinja evaluation, strings can be replaced by other types,
    68	    but we want to keep the original metadata for error reporting and source mapping.
    69	    For example, if a substitution replaces a string with a dictionary, we want that items
    70	    in the dictionary to still point to the original document location
    71	    """
    72	    if isinstance(value, ESPHomeDataBase):
    73	        return value
    74	    if isinstance(value, dict):
    75	        return {
    76	            _restore_data_base(k, orig_value): _restore_data_base(v, orig_value)
    77	            for k, v in value.items()
    78	        }
    79	    if isinstance(value, list):
    80	        return [_restore_data_base(v, orig_value) for v in value]
    81	    if isinstance(value, str):
    82	        return make_data_base(value, orig_value)
    83	    return value
    84

    86	def _resolve_var(name: str, context_vars: ContextVars) -> Any:
    87	    """Look up a substitution variable, falling back to the resolver callback."""
    88	    sub = context_vars.get(name, Missing)
    89	    if sub is Missing:
    90	        resolver = context_vars.get(Resolver)
    91	        if resolver:
    92	            sub = resolver(name)
    93	    return sub
    94	
    95	
    96	def _handle_undefined(
    97	    err: UndefinedError,
    98	    path: SubstitutionPath,
    99	    value: Any,
   100	    strict_undefined: bool,
   101	    errors: ErrList | None,
   102	) -> None:
   103	    """Handle an undefined variable.
   104	
   105	    In strict mode, raises immediately. Otherwise, appends to the errors
   106	    list for deferred warning at the end of the substitution pass.
   107	    """
   108	    if strict_undefined:
   109	        raise err
   110	    if errors is not None:
   111	        errors.append((err, path, value))
   112	
   113	
   114	def _expand_substitutions(
   115	    value: str,
   116	    path: SubstitutionPath,
   117	    context_vars: ContextVars,
   118	    strict_undefined: bool,
   119	    errors: ErrList | None,
   120	) -> Any:
   121	    """Expand ``$var``, ``${var}``, and Jinja expressions in a string.
   122	
   123	    Works in two phases:
   124	
   125	    1. **Simple substitution** — scan for ``$name`` / ``${name}`` tokens
   126	       and replace them with the value from *context_vars*.  If the token
   127	       spans the entire string, return the raw value (preserving type).
   128	    2. **Jinja evaluation** — if the result still contains Jinja syntax
   129	       (e.g. ``${a * b}``), render it through the Jinja engine with the
   130	       full *context_vars* as template variables.
   131	
   132	    Returns the expanded value (may be a non-string type) or the
   133	    original *value* unchanged if there is nothing to substitute.
   134	    """
   135	    if "$" not in value:
   136	        return value
   137	
   138	    orig_value = value
   139	
   140	    # Phase 1: Replace $var and ${var} references
   141	    search_pos = 0
   142	    while (m := cv.VARIABLE_PROG.search(value, search_pos)) is not None:
   143	        match_start, match_end = m.span(0)
   144	        name: str = m.group(1)
   145	        if name.startswith("{") and name.endswith("}"):
   146	            name = name[1:-1]
   147	        sub = _resolve_var(name, context_vars)
   148	        if sub is Missing:
   149	            _handle_undefined(
   150	                err=UndefinedError(f"'{name}' is undefined"),
   151	                path=path,
   152	                value=value,
   153	                strict_undefined=strict_undefined,
   154	                errors=errors,
   155	            )
   156	            search_pos = match_end
   157	            continue
   158	
   159	        if match_start == 0 and match_end == len(value):
   160	            # The variable spans the whole expression, e.g., "${varName}".
   161	            # Return its resolved value directly to conserve its type.
   162	            value = sub
   163	            break
   164	
   165	        tail = value[match_end:]
   166	        value = value[:match_start] + str(sub)
   167	        search_pos = len(value)
   168	        value += tail
   169	
   170	    # Phase 2: Evaluate any remaining jinja expressions (e.g., "${a * b}")
   171	    if isinstance(value, str) and has_jinja(value):
   172	        try:
   173	            value = jinja.expand(value, context_vars)
   174	        except UndefinedError as err:
   175	            _handle_undefined(
   176	                err=err,
   177	                path=path,
   178	                value=value,
   179	                strict_undefined=strict_undefined,
   180	                errors=errors,
   181	            )
   182	        except JinjaError as err:
   183	            raise cv.Invalid(
   184	                f"{err.error_name()} Error evaluating jinja expression"
   185	                f" '{value}': {str(err.parent())}."
   186	                f"\nEvaluation stack: (most recent evaluation last)"
   187	                f"\n{err.stack_trace_str()}"
   188	                f"\nRelevant context:\n{err.context_trace_str()}"
   189	                f"\nSee {'->'.join(str(x) for x in path)}",
   190	                path,
   191	            ) from err
   192	        else:
   193	            if isinstance(orig_value, ESPHomeDataBase):
   194	                value = _restore_data_base(value, orig_value)
   195	
   196	    # orig_value can also already be a lambda with esp_range info, and only
   197	    # a plain string is sent in orig_value
   198	    if isinstance(orig_value, ESPHomeDataBase):
   199	        # even though string can get larger or smaller, the range should point
   200	        # to original document marks
   201	        value = make_data_base(value, orig_value)
   202	
   203	    return value
   204	
   205	
   206	def _push_context(
   207	    local_vars: dict[str, Any],
   208	    parent_context: ContextVars,
   209	    errors: ErrList | None = None,
   210	) -> tuple[ContextVars, dict[str, Any]]:
   211	    """Resolve local_vars and layer them on top of parent_context.
   212	
   213	    Returns ``(child_context, resolved_vars)`` where *child_context* is a
   214	    new :class:`ChainMap` whose front map is *resolved_vars* (an
   215	    :class:`OrderedDict` of successfully-resolved variables).
   216	
   217	    Variables may reference each other (e.g. ``b: ${a + 1}``).
   218	    Dependencies are resolved recursively via a *resolver* callback
   219	    that Jinja invokes on cache-miss.  If vars are already in
   220	    dependency order, the loop iterates exactly once per variable.
   221	
   222	    The ChainMap stack used during resolution is::
   223	
   224	        resolver_context  →  resolved_vars  →  parent maps …
   225	              ↑                    ↑
   226	        holds Resolver       filled as vars
   227	        callback               are resolved
   228	    """
   229	    # Vars still waiting to be resolved — popped one-by-one by resolve().
   230	    unresolved_vars = local_vars.copy()
   231	    # Accumulates resolved values in dependency order; becomes the front
   232	    # map of the returned child context so later lookups find them first.
   233	    resolved_vars = OrderedDict()
   234	    # The context callees will search: resolved_vars (initially empty)
   235	    # shadowing whatever the parent already provides.
   236	    context_vars = parent_context.new_child(resolved_vars)
   237	
   238	    # Vars that failed resolution (missing or circular references).
   239	    # Maps name → (original_value, cause_error) for deferred warnings.
   240	    unresolvables: dict[str, tuple[Any, UndefinedError]] = {}
   241	
   242	    # One extra child layer so the Resolver callback lives in its own
   243	    # map and doesn't pollute resolved_vars.
   244	    resolver_context = context_vars.new_child()
   245	
   246	    def resolve(key: str) -> Any:
   247	        """Resolve a variable, recursively resolving any dependencies it references."""
   248	        value = unresolved_vars.pop(key, Missing)
   249	        if value is Missing:
   250	            return Missing
   251	        try:
   252	            value = substitute(value, [], resolver_context, True)
   253	        except UndefinedError as err:
   254	            unresolvables[key] = (value, err)
   255	            return Missing
   256	        resolved_vars[key] = value
   257	        return value
   258	
   259	    # Set up the resolver for use during substitution
   260	    resolver_context[Resolver] = resolve
   261	
   262	    # Resolve all variables, recursively resolving dependencies as needed.
   263	    # Each call to resolve() resolves that variable and any variables it depends on.
   264	    while unresolved_vars:
   265	        resolve(next(iter(unresolved_vars)))
   266	
   267	    for name, (value, cause) in unresolvables.items():
   268	        resolved_vars[name] = value
   269	        if errors is not None:
   270	            _handle_undefined(
   271	                err=UndefinedError(
   272	                    f"Could not resolve substitution variable '{name}': {cause}"
   273	                ),
   274	                path=["substitutions", name],
   275	                value=value,
   276	                strict_undefined=False,
   277	                errors=errors,
   278	            )
   279	
   280	    return context_vars, resolved_vars
   281	
   282	
   283	def push_context(
   284	    config_node: Any,
   285	    parent_context: ContextVars,
   286	    errors: ErrList | None = None,
   287	) -> ContextVars:
   288	    """Returns the context vars this config node must be evaluated with."""
   289	    if isinstance(config_node, ConfigContext):
   290	        return _push_context(config_node.vars, parent_context, errors)[0]
   291	
   292	    # This node does not define any vars itself, so just return parent context
   293	    return parent_context
   294	
   295	
   296	def resolve_include(
   297	    include: IncludeFile,
   298	    path: list[int | str],
   299	    context_vars: ContextVars,
   300	    strict_undefined: bool = True,
   301	    errors: ErrList | None = None,
   302	) -> tuple[Any, str]:
   303	    """Resolve an include, substituting the filename if needed.
   304	
   305	    Returns the loaded content and the resolved filename.
   306	
   307	    Note: no path-traversal validation is performed on the resolved filename.
   308	    A substitution that resolves to an absolute path will bypass the parent
   309	    directory (Path.__truediv__ ignores the left operand for absolute paths).
   310	    ESPHome's trust model assumes the config author controls all substitution
   311	    values (including command-line substitutions), so path restrictions are
   312	    an explicit non-goal here.
   313	    """
   314	    original = str(include.file)
   315	    filename = str(
   316	        _expand_substitutions(
   317	            original, path + ["file"], context_vars, strict_undefined, errors
   318	        )
   319	    )
   320	    if filename != original:
   321	        include = IncludeFile(
   322	            include.parent_file, filename, include.vars, include.yaml_loader
   323	        )
   324	    try:
   325	        return include.load(), filename
   326	    except esphome.core.EsphomeError as err:
   327	        raise cv.Invalid(
   328	            f"Error including file '{filename}': {err}",
   329	            path + [f"<{filename}>"],
   330	        ) from err
   331	
   332	
   333	def _substitute_include(
   334	    include: IncludeFile,
   335	    path: list[int | str],
   336	    context_vars: ContextVars,
   337	    strict_undefined: bool,
   338	    errors: ErrList | None,
   339	) -> Any:
   340	    """Resolve an include and substitute its content."""
   341	    content, filename = resolve_include(
   342	        include, path, context_vars, strict_undefined, errors
   343	    )
   344	    return substitute(
   345	        content, path + [f"<{filename}>"], context_vars, strict_undefined, errors
   346	    )
   347	
   348	
   349	def substitute(
   350	    item: Any,
   351	    path: SubstitutionPath,
   352	    parent_context: ContextVars,
   353	    strict_undefined: bool,
   354	    errors: ErrList | None = None,
   355	) -> Any:
   356	    """Returns a recursively substituted version of `item`."""
   357	
   358	    if isinstance(item, ESPLiteralValue):
   359	        return item  # do not substitute inside literal blocks
   360	
   361	    # Push the current item's context onto the context stack
   362	    context_vars = push_context(item, parent_context, errors)
   363	
   364	    result = item
   365	
   366	    if isinstance(item, list):
   367	        result = [
   368	            substitute(it, path + [i], context_vars, strict_undefined, errors)
   369	            for i, it in enumerate(item)
   370	        ]
   371	
   372	    elif isinstance(item, dict):
   373	        result = OrderedDict()
   374	        for k, v in item.items():
   375	            v = substitute(v, path + [k], context_vars, strict_undefined, errors)
   376	            k = substitute(k, path + [k], context_vars, strict_undefined, errors)
   377	            result[k] = merge_config(result.get(k), v)
   378	
   379	    elif isinstance(item, str):
   380	        result = _expand_substitutions(
   381	            item, path, context_vars, strict_undefined, errors
   382	        )
   383	
   384	    elif isinstance(item, (core.Lambda, Extend, Remove)) and item.value:
   385	        value = _expand_substitutions(
   386	            item.value, path, context_vars, strict_undefined, errors
   387	        )
   388	        if item.value != value:
   389	            result = type(item)(value)
   390	
   391	    elif isinstance(item, IncludeFile):
   392	        result = _substitute_include(item, path, context_vars, strict_undefined, errors)
   393	
   394	    if isinstance(item, ESPHomeDataBase):
   395	        result = make_data_base(result, item)
   396	    return result
   397	
   398	
   399	def _warn_unresolved_variables(errors: ErrList) -> None:
   400	    """Log warnings for unresolved substitution variables, skipping password fields."""
   401	    for err, path, expression in errors:
   402	        if "password" in path:
   403	            continue
   404	        location: str = "->".join(str(x) for x in path)
   405	        if isinstance(expression, ESPHomeDataBase) and expression.esp_range is not None:
   406	            location += f" in {str(expression.esp_range.start_mark)}"
   407	
   408	        _LOGGER.warning(
   409	            "The string '%s' looks like an expression,"
   410	            " but could not resolve all the variables: %s (see %s)",
   411	            expression,
   412	            err.message,
   413	            location,
   414	        )
   415	
   416	
   417	def do_substitution_pass(
   418	    config: OrderedDict, command_line_substitutions: dict[str, Any] | None = None
   419	) -> OrderedDict:
   420	    """Run the substitution pass over the entire config.
   421	
   422	    Extracts the ``substitutions:`` block, merges in any command-line
   423	    overrides, resolves inter-variable dependencies, then walks the
   424	    config tree replacing all ``$var`` / ``${expr}`` references.
   425	    Returns a new config dict with resolved substitutions
   426	    restored at the front.
   427	    """
   428	    # Extract substitutions from config, overriding with substitutions coming from command line:
   429	    # Use merge_dicts_ordered to preserve OrderedDict type for move_to_end()
   430	    substitutions = config.pop(CONF_SUBSTITUTIONS, {})
   431	    with cv.prepend_path(CONF_SUBSTITUTIONS):
   432	        if not isinstance(substitutions, dict):
   433	            raise cv.Invalid(
   434	                f"Substitutions must be a key to value mapping, got {type(substitutions)}"
   435	            )
   436	        substitutions = merge_dicts_ordered(
   437	            substitutions, command_line_substitutions or {}
   438	        )
   439	
   440	        replace_keys: list[tuple[str, str]] = []
   441	        for key in substitutions:
   442	            with cv.prepend_path(key):
   443	                sub = validate_substitution_key(key)
   444	                if sub != key:
   445	                    replace_keys.appe<response clipped><NOTE>To save on context only part of this file has been shown to you. You should retry this tool after you have searched inside the file with `grep -n` in order to find the line numbers of what you are looking for.</NOTE>

   417	def do_substitution_pass(
   418	    config: OrderedDict, command_line_substitutions: dict[str, Any] | None = None
   419	) -> OrderedDict:
   420	    """Run the substitution pass over the entire config.
   421	
   422	    Extracts the ``substitutions:`` block, merges in any command-line
   423	    overrides, resolves inter-variable dependencies, then walks the
   424	    config tree replacing all ``$var`` / ``${expr}`` references.
   425	    Returns a new config dict with resolved substitutions
   426	    restored at the front.
   427	    """
   428	    # Extract substitutions from config, overriding with substitutions coming from command line:
   429	    # Use merge_dicts_ordered to preserve OrderedDict type for move_to_end()
   430	    substitutions = config.pop(CONF_SUBSTITUTIONS, {})
   431	    with cv.prepend_path(CONF_SUBSTITUTIONS):
   432	        if not isinstance(substitutions, dict):
   433	            raise cv.Invalid(
   434	                f"Substitutions must be a key to value mapping, got {type(substitutions)}"
   435	            )
   436	        substitutions = merge_dicts_ordered(
   437	            substitutions, command_line_substitutions or {}
   438	        )
   439	
   440	        replace_keys: list[tuple[str, str]] = []
   441	        for key in substitutions:
   442	            with cv.prepend_path(key):
   443	                sub = validate_substitution_key(key)
   444	                if sub != key:
   445	                    replace_keys.append((key, sub))
   446	        for old, new in replace_keys:
   447	            substitutions[new] = substitutions[old]
   448	            del substitutions[old]
   449	
   450	    errors: ErrList = []  # Collect undefined errors during substitution
   451	    parent_context, substitutions = _push_context(substitutions, ContextVars(), errors)
   452	
   453	    config = substitute(config, [], parent_context, False, errors)
   454	
   455	    if errors:
   456	        _warn_unresolved_variables(errors)
   457	
   458	    # Restore substitutions to front of dict for readability
   459	    if substitutions:
   460	        config[CONF_SUBSTITUTIONS] = substitutions
   461	        config.move_to_end(CONF_SUBSTITUTIONS, last=False)
   462	    return config
   463

   151	        # pylint: disable=attribute-defined-outside-init
   152	        self._context_vars = vars
   153	
   154	    def copy_context_to_children(self) -> None:
   155	        """Propagate context to children.
   156	
   157	        isinstance(self, dict/list) works because ConfigContext is dynamically
   158	        mixed into dict/list subclasses via add_class_to_obj in add_context().
   159	        """
   160	        if isinstance(self, dict):
   161	            # pylint: disable=no-member
   162	            tagged = {
   163	                add_context(k, self.vars): add_context(v, self.vars)
   164	                for k, v in self.items()
   165	            }
   166	            self.clear()
   167	            self.update(tagged)
   168	        elif isinstance(self, list):
   169	            for i, item in enumerate(self):
   170	                # pylint: disable=unsupported-assignment-operation
   171	                self[i] = add_context(item, self.vars)

   174	_UNSET = object()
   175	
   176	
   177	class IncludeFile:
   178	    """Deferred !include that is resolved during the substitution pass.
   179	
   180	    Created during YAML parsing instead of loading the file immediately,
   181	    allowing substitution variables to appear in the filename path
   182	    (e.g. ``!include device-${platform}.yaml``). The actual file is
   183	    loaded on the first call to ``load()``, and the result is cached.
   184	    """
   185	
   186	    def __init__(
   187	        self,
   188	        parent_file: Path,
   189	        file: Path | str,
   190	        vars: dict[str, Any] | None,
   191	        yaml_loader: Callable[[Path], Any],
   192	    ) -> None:
   193	        self.parent_file = parent_file
   194	        self.file = Path(file)
   195	        self.vars = vars
   196	        self.yaml_loader = yaml_loader
   197	        self._content: Any = _UNSET
   198	
   199	    def __repr__(self) -> str:
   200	        return f"IncludeFile({self.file.as_posix()})"
   201	
   202	    def load(self) -> Any:
   203	        """Load and cache the included file content.
   204	
   205	        Note: returns the cached mutable object on subsequent calls.
   206	        Callers that need to modify the result should copy it first.
   207	        """
   208	        if self._content is not _UNSET:
   209	            return self._content
   210	        if self.has_unresolved_expressions():
   211	            from esphome.config_validation import Invalid
   212	
   213	            raise Invalid(
   214	                f"Cannot load include with unresolved substitutions: {self.file}"
   215	            )
   216	        self._content = self.yaml_loader(Path(self.parent_file.parent / self.file))
   217	        self._content = add_context(self._content, self.vars)
   218	        return self._content
   219	
   220	    def has_unresolved_expressions(self) -> bool:
   221	        """Check if the filename contains substitution variables or Jinja expressions."""
   222	        return has_substitution_or_expression(str(self.file))
   223	
   224	
   225	def _add_data_ref(fn):
   226	    @functools.wraps(fn)
   227	    def wrapped(loader, node):
   228	        res = fn(loader, node)
   229	        # newer PyYAML versions use generators, resolve them
   230	        if inspect.isgenerator(res):
   231	            generator = res
   232	            res = next(generator)
   233	            # Let generator finish
   234	            for _ in generator:
   235	                pass
   236	        res = make_data_base(res)
   237	        if isinstance(res, ESPHomeDataBase):
   238	            res.from_node(node)
   239	        return res
   240	
   241	    return wrapped
   242	
   243	
   244	_MAX_MERGE_INCLUDE_DEPTH = 10
   245	
   246	
   247	def _resolve_merge_include(value: Any, node: yaml.Node, value_node: yaml.Node) -> Any:
   248	    """Resolve an IncludeFile (and chains) and propagate context for merge key handling."""
   249	    for _ in range(_MAX_MERGE_INCLUDE_DEPTH):
   250	        if not isinstance(value, IncludeFile):
   251	            break
   252	        if value.has_unresolved_expressions():
   253	            raise yaml.constructor.ConstructorError(
   254	                "While constructing a mapping",
   255	                node.start_mark,
   256	                "Substitution in include filename with merge keys is not supported yet.",
   257	                value_node.start_mark,
   258	            )
   259	        value = value.load()
   260	    else:
   261	        raise yaml.constructor.ConstructorError(
   262	            "While constructing a mapping",
   263	            node.start_mark,
   264	            f"Maximum include chain depth ({_MAX_MERGE_INCLUDE_DEPTH}) exceeded in merge key",
   265	            value_node.start_mark,
   266	        )
   267	    if isinstance(value, ConfigContext):
   268	        # Since the parent dict/list will disappear, propagate
   269	        # context to children now to retain context vars
   270	        value.copy_context_to_children()
   271	    return value

   432	        try:
   433	            secrets = self.yaml_loader(self._rel_path(SECRET_YAML))
   434	        except EsphomeError as e:

   452	    @_add_data_ref
   453	    def construct_include(self, node: yaml.Node) -> Any:
   454	        from esphome.const import CONF_VARS
   455	
   456	        def extract_file_vars(node):

   459	            if file is None:
   460	                raise yaml.MarkedYAMLError("Must include 'file'", node.start_mark)
   461	            vars = fields.get(CONF_VARS)

   469	        return IncludeFile(self.name, file, vars, self.yaml_loader)
   470	
   471	    # Directory includes (!include_dir_*) load eagerly during YAML parsing
   472	    # because their paths are directory names, not individual files, and
   473	    # substitutions in directory paths are not supported.
   474	
   475	    @_add_data_ref
   476	    def construct_include_dir_list(self, node: yaml.Node) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
   477	        files = filter_yaml_files(_find_files(self._rel_path(node.value), "*.yaml"))
   478	        return [self.yaml_loader(f) for f in files]
   479	
   480	    @_add_data_ref
   481	    def construct_include_dir_merge_list(self, node: yaml.Node) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
   482	        files = filter_yaml_files(_find_files(self._rel_path(node.value), "*.yaml"))
   483	        merged_list = []
   484	        for fname in files:
   485	            loaded_yaml = self.yaml_loader(fname)
   486	            if isinstance(loaded_yaml, list):
   487	                merged_list.extend(loaded_yaml)
   488	        return merged_list
   489	
   490	    @_add_data_ref
   491	    def construct_include_dir_named(
   492	        self, node: yaml.Node
   493	    ) -> OrderedDict[str, dict[str, Any]]:
   494	        files = filter_yaml_files(_find_files(self._rel_path(node.value), "*.yaml"))
   495	        mapping = OrderedDict()
   496	        for fname in files:
   497	            filename = fname.stem
   498	            mapping[filename] = self.yaml_loader(fname)
   499	        return mapping
   500	
   501	    @_add_data_ref
   502	    def construct_include_dir_merge_named(
   503	        self, node: yaml.Node
   504	    ) -> OrderedDict[str, dict[str, Any]]:
   505	        files = filter_yaml_files(_find_files(self._rel_path(node.value), "*.yaml"))
   506	        mapping = OrderedDict()
   507	        for fname in files:
   508	            loaded_yaml = self.yaml_loader(fname)
   509	            if isinstance(loaded_yaml, dict):
   510	                mapping.update(loaded_yaml)
   511	        return mapping
   512	
   513	    @_add_data_ref
   514	    def construct_lambda(self, node: yaml.Node) -> Lambda:
   515	        return Lambda(str(node.value))
   516	
   517	    @_add_data_ref
   518	    def construct_literal(self, node: yaml.Node) -> ESPLiteralValue:
   519	        obj = None
   520	        if isinstance(node, yaml.ScalarNode):
   521	            obj = self.construct_scalar(node)
   522	        elif isinstance(node, yaml.SequenceNode):
   523	            obj = self.construct_sequence(node)
   524	        elif isinstance(node, yaml.MappingNode):
   525	            obj = self.construct_mapping(node)
   526	        return add_class_to_obj(obj, ESPLiteralValue)
   527	
   528	    @_add_data_ref
   529	    def construct_extend(self, node: yaml.Node) -> Extend:
   530	        return Extend(str(node.value))
   531	
   532	    @_add_data_ref
   533	    def construct_remove(self, node: yaml.Node) -> Remove:
   534	        return Remove(str(node.value))
   535	
   536	
   537	class ESPHomeLoader(ESPHomeLoaderMixin, FastestAvailableSafeLoader):
   538	    """Loader class that keeps track of line numbers."""
   539	
   540	    def __init__(
   541	        self,
   542	        stream: TextIOBase | BytesIO,
   543	        name: Path,
   544	        yaml_loader: Callable[[Path], dict[str, Any]],
   545	    ) -> None:
   546	        FastestAvailableSafeLoader.__init__(self, stream)
   547	        ESPHomeLoaderMixin.__init__(self, name, yaml_loader)
   548	
   549	
   550	class ESPHomePurePythonLoader(ESPHomeLoaderMixin, PurePythonLoader):
   551	    """Loader class that keeps track of line numbers."""
   552	
   553	    def __init__(
   554	        self,
   555	        stream: TextIOBase | BytesIO,
   556	        name: Path,
   557	        yaml_loader: Callable[[Path], dict[str, Any]],
   558	    ) -> None:
   559	        PurePythonLoader.__init__(self, stream)
   560	        ESPHomeLoaderMixin.__init__(self, name, yaml_loader)
   561	
   562	
   563	for _loader in (ESPHomeLoader, ESPHomePurePythonLoader):
   564	    _loader.add_constructor("tag:yaml.org,2002:int", _loader.construct_yaml_int)
   565	    _loader.add_constructor("tag:yaml.org,2002:float", _loader.construct_yaml_float)
   566	    _loader.add_constructor("tag:yaml.org,2002:binary", _loader.construct_yaml_binary)
   567	    _loader.add_constructor("tag:yaml.org,2002:omap", _loader.construct_yaml_omap)
   568	    _loader.add_constructor("tag:yaml.org,2002:str", _loader.construct_yaml_str)
   569	    _loader.add_constructor("tag:yaml.org,2002:seq", _loader.construct_yaml_seq)
   570	    _loader.add_constructor("tag:yaml.org,2002:map", _loader.construct_yaml_map)
   571	    _loader.add_constructor("!env_var", _loader.construct_env_var)
   572	    _loader.add_constructor("!secret", _loader.construct_secret)
   573	    _loader.add_constructor("!include", _loader.construct_include)
   574	    _loader.add_constructor("!include_dir_list", _loader.construct_include_dir_list)
   575	    _loader.add_constructor(
   576	        "!include_dir_merge_list", _loader.construct_include_dir_merge_list

   578	    _loader.add_constructor("!include_dir_named", _loader.construct_include_dir_named)
   579	    _loader.add_constructor(
   580	        "!include_dir_merge_named", _loader.construct_include_dir_merge_named
   581	    )
   582	    _loader.add_constructor("!lambda", _loader.construct_lambda)
   583	    _loader.add_constructor("!literal", _loader.construct_literal)
   584	    _loader.add_constructor("!extend", _loader.construct_extend)
   585	    _loader.add_constructor("!remove", _loader.construct_remove)
   586	
   587	
   588	def load_yaml(fname: Path, clear_secrets: bool = True) -> Any:
   589	    if clear_secrets:
   590	        _SECRET_VALUES.clear()
   591	        _SECRET_CACHE.clear()
   592	    return _load_yaml_internal(fname)
   593	
   594	
   595	def _load_yaml_internal(fname: Path) -> Any:
   596	    """Load a YAML file."""
   597	    for listener in _load_listeners:
   598	        listener(fname)
   599	    try:
   600	        with fname.open(encoding="utf-8") as f_handle:
   601	            res = parse_yaml(fname, f_handle)
   602	    except (UnicodeDecodeError, OSError) as err:
   603	        raise EsphomeError(f"Error reading file {fname}: {err}") from err
   604	    # Top-level !include returns a deferred IncludeFile; resolve it so
   605	    # callers always receive the final content.
   606	    if isinstance(res, IncludeFile):
   607	        res = res.load()
   608	    return res
   609	
   610	
   611	def parse_yaml(file_name: Path, file_handle: TextIOWrapper, yaml_loader=None) -> Any:
   612	    """Parse a YAML file."""
   613	    if yaml_loader is None:
   614	        yaml_loader = _load_yaml_internal
   615	    try:
   616	        return _load_yaml_internal_with_type(
   617	            ESPHomeLoader, file_name, file_handle, yaml_loader
   618	        )
   619	    except EsphomeError:
   620	        # Loading failed, so we now load with the Python loader which has more
   621	        # readable exceptions
   622	        # Rewind the stream so we can try again
   623	        file_handle.seek(0, 0)
   624	        return _load_yaml_internal_with_type(
   625	            ESPHomePurePythonLoader, file_name, file_handle, yaml_loader

from pathlib import Path
from tempfile import TemporaryDirectory
from esphome import yaml_util
from esphome.components import substitutions

with TemporaryDirectory() as d:
    root = Path(d)
    (root / 'mydevice.yaml').write_text('''substitutions: !include subs.yaml\nesphome:\n  name: test-device\nvalue: ${my_variable}\n''')

   308	    @_add_data_ref
   309	    def construct_yaml_map(self, node: yaml.MappingNode) -> OrderedDict[str, Any]:
   310	        """Traverses the given mapping node and returns a list of constructed key-value pairs."""
   311	        assert isinstance(node, yaml.MappingNode)
   312	        # A list of key-value pairs we find in the current mapping
   313	        pairs = []
   314	        # A list of key-value pairs we find while resolving merges ('<<' key), will be
   315	        # added to pairs in a second pass
   316	        merge_pairs = []
   317	        # A dict of seen keys so far, used to alert the user of duplicate keys and checking
   318	        # which keys to merge.
   319	        # Value of dict items is the start mark of the previous declaration.
   320	        seen_keys = {}
   321	
   322	        for key_node, value_node in node.value:
   323	            # merge key is '<<'
   324	            is_merge_key = key_node.tag == "tag:yaml.org,2002:merge"
   325	            # key has no explicit tag set
   326	            is_default_tag = key_node.tag == "tag:yaml.org,2002:value"
   327	
   328	            if is_default_tag:
   329	                # Default tag for mapping keys is string
   330	                key_node.tag = "tag:yaml.org,2002:str"
   331	
   332	            if not is_merge_key:
   333	                # base case, this is a simple key-value pair
   334	                key = self.construct_object(key_node)
   335	                value = self.construct_object(value_node)
   336	
   337	                # Check if key is hashable
   338	                try:
   339	                    hash(key)
   340	                except TypeError:
   341	                    raise yaml.constructor.ConstructorError(
   342	                        f'Invalid key "{key}" (not hashable)', key_node.start_mark
   343	                    ) from None
   344	
   345	                key = make_data_base(str(key))
   346	                key.from_node(key_node)
   347	
   348	                # Check if it is a duplicate key
   349	                if key in seen_keys:
   350	                    raise yaml.constructor.ConstructorError(
   351	                        f'Duplicate key "{key}"',
   352	                        key_node.start_mark,
   353	                        "NOTE: Previous declaration here:",
   354	                        seen_keys[key],
   355	                    )
   356	                seen_keys[key] = key_node.start_mark
   357	
   358	                # Add to pairs
   359	                pairs.append((key, value))
   360	                continue
   361	
   362	            # This is a merge key, resolve value and add to merge_pairs
   363	            value = self.construct_object(value_node)
   364	
   365	            value = _resolve_merge_include(value, node, value_node)
   366	
   367	            if isinstance(value, dict):
   368	                # base case, copy directly to merge_pairs
   369	                # direct merge, like "<<: {some_key: some_value}"
   370	                merge_pairs.extend(value.items())
   371	            elif isinstance(value, list):
   372	                # sequence merge, like "<<: [{some_key: some_value}, {other_key: some_value}]"
   373	                for item in value:
   374	                    item = _resolve_merge_include(item, node, value_node)
   375	                    if not isinstance(item, dict):
   376	                        raise yaml.constructor.ConstructorError(
   377	                            "While constructing a mapping",
   378	                            node.start_mark,
   379	                            f"Expected a mapping for merging, but found {type(item)}",
   380	                            value_node.start_mark,
   381	                        )
   382	                    merge_pairs.extend(item.items())
   383	            else:
   384	                raise yaml.constructor.ConstructorError(
   385	                    "While constructing a mapping",
   386	                    node.start_mark,
   387	                    f"Expected a mapping or list of mappings for merging, but found {type(value)}",
   388	                    value_node.start_mark,
   389	                )
   390	
   391	        if merge_pairs:
   392	            # We found some merge keys along the way, merge them into base pairs
   393	            # https://yaml.org/type/merge.html
   394	            # Construct a new merge set with values overridden by current mapping or earlier
   395	            # sequence entries removed
   396	            for key, value in merge_pairs:
   397	                if key in seen_keys:
   398	                    # key already in the current map or from an earlier merge sequence entry,
   399	                    # do not override
   400	                    #
   401	                    # "... each of its key/value pairs is inserted into the current mapping,
   402	                    # unless the key already exists in it."
   403	                    #
   404	                    # "If the value associated with the merge key is a sequence, then this sequence
   405	                    #  is expected to contain mapping nodes and each of these nodes is merged in
   406	                    #  turn according to its order in the sequence. Keys in mapping nodes earlier
   407	                    #  in the sequence override keys specified in later mapping nodes."
   408	                    continue
   409	                pairs.append((key, value))
   410	                # Add key node to seen keys, for sequence merge values.
   411	                seen_keys[key] = None
   412	
   413	        return OrderedDict(pairs)
   414	
   415	    @_add_data_ref
   416	    def construct_env_var(self, node: yaml.Node) -> str:
   417	        args = node.value.split()
   418	        # Check for a default value
   419	        if len(args) > 1:
   420	            return os.getenv(args[0], " ".join(args[1:]))
   421	        if args[0] in os.environ:

   114	def add_context(value: Any, context_vars: dict[str, Any] | None) -> Any:
   115	    """Tags a list/string/dict value with context vars that must be applied to it and its children
   116	    during the substitution pass. If no vars are given, no tagging is done.
   117	    If the value is already tagged, the new context vars are merged with existing ones,
   118	    with new vars taking precedence. Returns the value tagged with ConfigContext. Returns
   119	    the original value if value is not a list/string/dict.
   120	    """
   121	    if isinstance(value, dict) and CONF_DEFAULTS in value:
   122	        context_vars = {
   123	            **value.pop(CONF_DEFAULTS),
   124	            **(context_vars or {}),
   125	        }
   126	
   127	    if isinstance(value, ConfigContext):
   128	        value.set_context({**value.vars, **(context_vars or {})})
   129	        return value
   130	
   131	    if context_vars and isinstance(value, (dict, list, str)):
   132	        value = add_class_to_obj(value, ConfigContext)
   133	        value.set_context(context_vars)
   134	    return value
   135	
   136	
   137	class ConfigContext:
   138	    """This is a mixin class that holds substitution vars that should be applied
   139	    to the tagged node and its children. During configuration loading, context vars can
   140	    be added to nodes using `add_context` function, which applies the mixin storing
   141	    the captured values and unevaluated expressions.
   142	    The substitution pass then recreates the effective context by merging the context vars
   143	    from this node and parent nodes.
   144	    """
   145	
   146	    @property
   147	    def vars(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
   148	        return self._context_vars

   301	) -> None:
   302	    """Iterate a packages list in reverse priority order, invoking callback on each entry."""
   303	    for idx in reversed(range(len(packages))):
   304	        with cv.prepend_path(idx):
   305	            packages[idx] = callback(packages[idx], context)
   306	
   307	
   308	def _walk_packages(
   309	    config: dict,
   310	    callback: Callable[[dict, ContextVars | None], dict],
   311	    context: ContextVars | None = None,
   312	    validate_deprecated: bool = True,
   313	) -> dict:
   314	    """Walks the packages structure in priority order, invoking ``callback`` on each package definition found.
   315	
   316	    This function only iterates over the immediate ``packages:`` entries in *config*.
   317	    If packages may contain nested ``packages:`` keys, the *callback* is responsible
   318	    for recursing by calling ``_walk_packages`` on the returned package config.
   319	    """
   320	    if CONF_PACKAGES not in config:
   321	        return config
   322	    packages = config[CONF_PACKAGES]
   323	
   324	    with cv.prepend_path(CONF_PACKAGES):
   325	        if isinstance(packages, yaml_util.IncludeFile):
   326	            # If the packages key is an IncludeFile, resolve it first before processing.
   327	            packages, _ = resolve_include(packages, [], context, strict_undefined=False)
   328	        if not isinstance(packages, (dict, list)):
   329	            raise cv.Invalid(
   330	                f"Packages must be a key to value mapping or list, got {type(packages)} instead"
   331	            )
   332	
   333	        if not isinstance(packages, dict):
   334	            _walk_package_list(packages, callback, context)
   335	        elif (result := _walk_package_dict(packages, callback, context)) is not None:
   336	            if not validate_deprecated or any(
   337	                is_package_definition(v) for v in packages.values()
   338	            ):
   339	                raise result
   340	            # Fallback: treat the dict as a single deprecated package.
   341	            # This block can be removed once the single-package
   342	            # deprecation period (2026.7.0) is over.
   343	            config[CONF_PACKAGES] = [packages]
   344	            return _walk_packages(deprecate_single_package(config), callback, context)
   345	
   346	    config[CONF_PACKAGES] = packages
   347	    return config
   348	
   349	
   350	def _substitute_package_definition(
   351	    package_config: dict | str, context_vars: ContextVars | None
   352	) -> dict | str:
   353	    """Substitute variables in a package definition string or remote package dict.
   354	
   355	    Only substitutes strings and remote package dicts (URLs, refs, paths).
   356	    Local package contents are left untouched — they will be substituted
   357	    later during the main substitution pass.
   358	    """
   359	    if isinstance(package_config, str) or (
   360	        isinstance(package_config, dict) and is_remote_package(package_config)
   361	    ):
   362	        package_config = substitute(
   363	            item=package_config,
   364	            path=[],
   365	            parent_context=context_vars or ContextVars(),
   366	            strict_undefined=False,
   367	        )
   368	    return package_config
   369	
   370	
   371	def _update_substitutions_context(
   372	    parent_context: UserDict,
   373	    package_substitutions: dict[str, Any],
   374	) -> None:
   375	    """Resolve and add new substitutions to the parent context.
   376	
   377	    Skips keys already present (higher-priority sources win).
   378	    String values are substituted against the current context so that
   379	    cross-references between substitutions are expanded when possible.
   380	    """
   381	    for key, value in package_substitutions.items():
   382	        if key in parent_context:
   383	            continue
   384	        if not isinstance(value, str):
   385	            parent_context[key] = value
   386	            continue
   387	        parent_context[key] = substitute(
   388	            item=value,
   389	            path=[CONF_SUBSTITUTIONS, key],
   390	            parent_context=ContextVars(parent_context),
   391	            strict_undefined=False,
   392	        )
   393	
   394	
   395	class _PackageProcessor:
   396	    """Stateful processor that resolves packages and collects substitutions.
   397	
   398	    Packages are processed highest-priority first (later-declared before
   399	    earlier-declared) so that their substitutions are available when
   400	    resolving lower-priority package definitions.  For each entry:
   401	
   402	    1. Substitute variables in remote package definitions (URLs, refs, paths).
   403	    2. Validate against ``PACKAGE_SCHEMA`` and download remote packages.
   404	    3. Extract ``substitutions:`` and merge into the shared context
   405	       (higher-priority packages win on conflicts).
   406	    4. Recurse into any nested ``packages:`` keys.
   407	
   408	    Command-line substitutions take the highest priority and are never overridden.
   409	    """
   410	
   411	    def __init__(
   412	        self,
   413	        substitutions: UserDict,
   414	        command_line_substitutions: dict[str, Any] | None,
   415	        skip_update: bool,
   416	    ) -> None:
   417	        self.substitutions = substitutions
   418	        self.parent_context = UserDict(command_line_substitutions or {})
   419	        self.skip_update = skip_update
   420	
   421	    def resolve_package(
   422	        self,
   423	        package_config: dict | str | yaml_util.IncludeFile,
   424	        context_vars: ContextVars | None,
   425	    ) -> dict:
   426	        """Resolve a package definition to a concrete ``dict`` and fetch remote packages.
   427	
   428	        The input may be a ``str`` (git shorthand or Jinja expression), a
   429	        ``dict`` (remote or local package), or an ``IncludeFile`` whose filename
   430	        may itself contain substitution expressions.
   431	
   432	        The loop handles the case where loading an ``IncludeFile`` yields another
   433	        ``IncludeFile`` (e.g. a chain of deferred includes).  Each iteration:
   434	
   435	        1. If the current value is an ``IncludeFile``, load it — resolving any
   436	           substitutions in its filename first.
   437	        2. Substitute variables in the resulting value (for strings and remote
   438	           package dicts).
   439	        3. Validate against ``PACKAGE_SCHEMA``.  If the result is a ``dict``,
   440	           the loop exits; otherwise another iteration is needed.
   441	
   442	        Raises ``cv.Invalid`` if the chain has not resolved to a ``dict`` after
   443	        ``MAX_INCLUDE_DEPTH`` iterations.
   444	        """
   445	        for _ in range(MAX_INCLUDE_DEPTH):
   446	            if isinstance(package_config, yaml_util.IncludeFile):
   447	                package_config, _ = resolve_include(
   448	                    package_config,
   449	                    [],
   450	                    context_vars or ContextVars(),
   451	                    strict_undefined=False,
   452	                )
   453	
   454	            package_config = _substitute_package_definition(
   455	                package_config, context_vars
   456	            )
   457	            package_config = PACKAGE_SCHEMA(package_config)
   458	            if isinstance(package_config, dict):
   459	                break
   460	        else:
   461	            raise cv.Invalid(
   462	                f"Maximum include nesting depth ({MAX_INCLUDE_DEPTH}) exceeded"
   463	            )
   464	
   465	        if is_remote_package(package_config):
   466	            package_config = _process_remote_package(package_config, self.skip_update)
   467	        return package_config
   468	
   469	    def collect_substitutions(self, package_config: dict) -> None:
   470	        """Extract substitutions from a package and merge into the shared context."""

    45	def ensure_unique_string(preferred_string, current_strings):
    46	    test_string = preferred_string
    47	    current_strings_set = set(current_strings)
    48	
    49	    tries = 1
    50	
    51	    while test_string in current_strings_set:
    52	        tries += 1
    53	        test_string = f"{preferred_string}_{tries}"
    54	
    55	    return test_string
    56	
    57	
    58	def fnv1_hash(string: str) -> int:
    59	    """FNV-1 32-bit hash function (multiply then XOR)."""
    60	    hash_value = FNV1_OFFSET_BASIS
    61	    for char in string:
    62	        hash_value = (hash_value * FNV1_PRIME) & 0xFFFFFFFF
    63	        hash_value ^= ord(char)
    64	    return hash_value
    65	
    66	
    67	def fnv1a_32bit_hash(string: str) -> int:
    68	    """FNV-1a 32-bit hash function (XOR then multiply).
    69	
    70	    Note: This uses 32-bit hash instead of 64-bit for several reasons:
    71	    1. ESPHome targets 32-bit microcontrollers with limited RAM (often <320KB)
    72	    2. Using 64-bit hashes would double the RAM usage for storing IDs
    73	    3. 64-bit operations are slower on 32-bit processors
    74	
    75	    While there's a ~50% collision probability at ~77,000 unique IDs,
    76	    ESPHome validates for collisions at compile time, preventing any
    77	    runtime issues. In practice, most ESPHome installations only have
    78	    a handful of area_ids and device_ids (typically <10 areas and <100
    79	    devices), making collisions virtually impossible.
    80	    """
    81	    hash_value = FNV1_OFFSET_BASIS
    82	    for char in string:
    83	        hash_value ^= ord(char)
    84	        hash_value = (hash_value * FNV1_PRIME) & 0xFFFFFFFF
    85	    return hash_value
    86	
    87	
    88	def fnv1_hash_object_id(name: str) -> int:
    89	    """Compute FNV-1 hash of name with snake_case + sanitize transformations.
    90	
    91	    IMPORTANT: Must produce same result as C++ fnv1_hash_object_id() in helpers.h.
    92	    Used for pre-computing entity object_id hashes at code generation time.
    93	    """
    94	    return fnv1_hash(sanitize(snake_case(name)))

    99	    import unicodedata
   100	
   101	    return "".join(
   102	        c
   103	        for c in unicodedata.normalize("NFD", str(value))
   104	        if unicodedata.category(c) != "Mn"
   105	    )

   108	def slugify(value: str) -> str:
   109	    """Convert a string to a valid C++ identifier slug."""
   110	    from esphome.const import ALLOWED_NAME_CHARS
   111	
   112	    value = (
   113	        strip_accents(value)
   114	        .lower()
   115	        .replace(" ", "_")
   116	        .replace("-", "_")
   117	        .replace("__", "_")
   118	        .strip("_")
   119	    )
   120	    return "".join(c for c in value if c in ALLOWED_NAME_CHARS)

   477	    ) -> dict:
   478	        """Resolve a single package and recurse into any nested packages."""
   479	        from_remote = isinstance(package_config, dict) and is_remote_package(
   480	            package_config
   481	        )
   482	        package_config = self.resolve_package(package_config, context_vars)
   483	        self.collect_substitutions(package_config)

   489	        context_vars = push_context(package_config, context_vars)
   490	        context_vars = push_context(package_config[CONF_PACKAGES], context_vars)
   491	        # Disable the deprecated single-package fallback for remote
   492	        # packages.  _process_remote_package returns dicts with
   493	        # already-resolved values that is_package_definition cannot
   494	        # distinguish from config fragments, so the fallback would
   495	        # always fire and mask real errors with wrong paths
   496	        # (packages->0 instead of packages-><name>).
   497	        return _walk_packages(
   498	            package_config,
   499	            self.process_package,
   500	            context_vars,

   544	    Must be called after :func:`do_packages_pass` has resolved all packages.
   545	    """

   547	        return config

   556	        merge_list.append(package_config)
   557	        return _walk_packages(package_config, process_package_callback)

   531	
   532	# A dict of types that need to be converted to heaptypes before a class can be added
   533	# to the object
   534	_TYPE_OVERLOADS = {
   535	    int: type("EInt", (int,), {}),
   536	    float: type("EFloat", (float,), {}),
   537	    str: type("EStr", (str,), {}),
   538	    dict: type("EDict", (dict,), {}),
   539	    list: type("EList", (list,), {}),
   540	}
   541	
   542	# cache created classes here
   543	_CLASS_LOOKUP = {}
   544	
   545	
   546	def add_class_to_obj(value, cls):
   547	    """Add a class to a python type.
   548	
   549	    This function modifies value so that it has cls as a basetype.
   550	    The value itself may be modified by this action! You must use the return
   551	    value of this function however, since some types need to be copied first (heaptypes).
   552	    """
   553	    if isinstance(value, cls):
   554	        # If already is instance, do not add
   555	        return value
   556	
   557	    try:
   558	        orig_cls = value.__class__
   559	        key = (orig_cls, cls)
   560	        new_cls = _CLASS_LOOKUP.get(key)
   561	        if new_cls is None:
   562	            new_cls = orig_cls.__class__(orig_cls.__name__, (orig_cls, cls), {})
   563	            _CLASS_LOOKUP[key] = new_cls
   564	        value.__class__ = new_cls
   565	        return value
   566	    except TypeError:
   567	        # Non heap type, look in overloads dict
   568	        for type_, func in _TYPE_OVERLOADS.items():
   569	            # Use type() here, we only need to trigger if it's the exact type,
   570	            # as otherwise we don't need to overload the class
   571	            if type(value) is type_:  # pylint: disable=unidiomatic-typecheck
   572	                return add_class_to_obj(func(value), cls)
   573	        raise
   574

20:def merge_dicts_ordered(*dicts: dict) -> OrderedDict:
from collections.abc import Callable

from esphome.const import (
    CONF_LEVEL,
    CONF_LOGGER,
    KEY_CORE,
    KEY_TARGET_FRAMEWORK,
    KEY_TARGET_PLATFORM,
    PlatformFramework,
)
from esphome.core import CORE
from esphome.util import OrderedDict

# Pre-build lookup map from (platform, framework) tuples to PlatformFramework enum
_PLATFORM_FRAMEWORK_LOOKUP = {
    (pf.value[0].value, pf.value[1].value): pf for pf in PlatformFramework
}


def merge_dicts_ordered(*dicts: dict) -> OrderedDict:
    """Merge multiple dicts into an OrderedDict, preserving key order.

    This is a helper to ensure that dictionary merging preserves OrderedDict type,
    which is important for operations like move_to_end().

    Args:
        *dicts: Variable number of dictionaries to merge (later dicts override earlier ones)

    Returns:
        OrderedDict with merged contents
    """
    result = OrderedDict()
    for d in dicts:
        if d:
            result.update(d)
    return result


class Extend:
    def __init__(self, value):
        self.value = value

    def __str__(self):
        return f"!extend {self.value}"

    def __repr__(self):
        return f"Extend({self.value})"

    def __eq__(self, b):
        """
        Check if two Extend objects contain the same ID.

        Only used in unit tests.
        """
        return isinstance(b, Extend) and self.value == b.value


class Remove:
    def __init__(self, value=None):
        self.value = value

    def __str__(self):
        return f"!remove {self.value}"

    def __repr__(self):
        return f"Remove({self.value})"

    def __eq__(self, b):
        """
        Check if two Remove objects contain the same ID.

        Only used in unit tests.
        """
        return isinstance(b, Remove) and self.value == b.value


def merge_config(old, new):
    if isinstance(new, Remove):
        return new
    if isinstance(new, dict):
        if not isinstance(old, dict):
            return new
        # Preserve OrderedDict type by copying to OrderedDict if either input is OrderedDict
        if isinstance(old, OrderedDict) or isinstance(new, OrderedDict):
            res = OrderedDict(old)
        else:
            res = old.copy()
        for k, v in new.items():
            res[k] = merge_config(old.get(k), v)
        return res
    if isinstance(new, list):
        if not isinstance(old, list):
            return new
        return old + new
    if new is None:
        return old

    return new


def filter_source_files_from_platform(
    files_map: dict[str, set[PlatformFramework]],
) -> Callable[[], list[str]]:

                  that should compile this file

        Function that returns list of files to exclude for current platform
    """

        core_data = CORE.data.get(KEY_CORE, {})
        target_platform = core_data.get(KEY_TARGET_PLATFORM)
        target_framework = core_data.get(KEY_TARGET_FRAMEWORK)

        if not target_platform or not target_framework:

from pathlib import Path
from tempfile import TemporaryDirectory
from esphome import yaml_util
from esphome.components.packages import do_packages_pass
from esphome.components import substitutions

with TemporaryDirectory() as d:
    root = Path(d)
    (root / 'main.yaml').write_text('''substitutions: !include subs.yaml\npackages: {}\nvalue: ${my_variable}\n''')
    (root / 'subs.yaml').write_text('my_variable: "hello"\n')
    config = yaml_util.load_yaml(root / 'main.yaml')
    try:
        config = do_packages_pass(config)
        config = substitutions.do_substitution_pass(config)
        print('value:', config['value'])
    except Exception as e:
        print(type(e).__name__, e)
        raise

        """Extract substitutions from a package and merge into the shared context."""
        if subs := package_config.pop(CONF_SUBSTITUTIONS, {}):
            with cv.prepend_path(CONF_SUBSTITUTIONS):
                if isinstance(subs, yaml_util.IncludeFile):

   469	    def collect_substitutions(self, package_config: dict) -> None:
   470	        """Extract substitutions from a package and merge into the shared context."""
   471	        if subs := package_config.pop(CONF_SUBSTITUTIONS, {}):
   472	            with cv.prepend_path(CONF_SUBSTITUTIONS):
   473	                if isinstance(subs, yaml_util.IncludeFile):
   474	                    subs, _ = resolve_include(
   475	                        subs,
   476	                        [],
   477	                        ContextVars(self.parent_context),
   478	                        strict_undefined=False,
   479	                    )
   480	                if not isinstance(subs, dict):
   481	                    raise cv.Invalid(
   482	                        f"Substitutions must be a key to value mapping, got {type(subs)}"
   483	                    )
   484	            self.substitutions.data = merge_config(subs, self.substitutions.data)
   485	            _update_substitutions_context(self.parent_context, subs)
   486	
   487	    def process_package(
   488	        self, package_config: dict | str, context_vars: ContextVars | None
   489	    ) -> dict:
Review the changes and make sure they are as expected. Edit the file again if necessary.

from pathlib import Path
from tempfile import TemporaryDirectory
from esphome import yaml_util
from esphome.components import substitutions

with TemporaryDirectory() as d:
    root = Path(d)
    (root / 'project').mkdir()
    (root / 'shared').mkdir()
    (root / 'project' / 'components').mkdir()

+            # substitutions block must be loaded first so it can seed that walk.
+            substitutions, _ = resolve_include(
+                substitutions,
+                [],
+                ContextVars(command_line_substitutions or {}),
+                strict_undefined=False,
+                errors=errors,
+            )
         if not isinstance(substitutions, dict):
             raise cv.Invalid(
                 f"Substitutions must be a key to value mapping, got {type(substitutions)}"
